Highly recommend this place for acupuncture!! Sappho was so incredibly helpful in every way. I started seeing her once a week for my chronic illness and she had a wonderfully calming presence, was so full of insight and information on what points effected which organs and how they work in conjunction with my fatigue and pain. She gave me useful tips and suggestions for nutrition and health supplements and was always so gentle when treating me. I was having issues with my blood flow and regular periods, and immediately one day after seeing Sappho I got my period and reset my body! I was so thankful that they took my insurance and treated me with such kindness as a patient. I felt so much better after a few months of going to Sappho, I wish I still lived in the area to go to her every week!!<//text>

1436377286616</Time>
< rate>
1< /rate>
< Text>
Several years ago, we hired this company as a second estimate on replacing a complete HVAC system.  We were very happy with their price and the quickness of installation.
One year later, the coil unit they installed went out.  I called them, and because the installation was still under warranty, they replaced the part free of charge.
Two years later....the same part went out again.  We called another company (more local to us) to inspect.  They determined that not only was the part faulty, and that this model has a long history of complaints, but that the workmanship done in the attic was so poorly done that it was a hazard, and the entire system would need to be overhauled at nearly the cost of a complete new unit.

I called Dependable to see if there was anything they could do. The woman on the phone was very rude and emphatic that the warranty was expired.  I told her this is the second time this part has completely failed in 5 years. We had confirmation there is something wrong with the part they installed, AND the workmanship, and shouldn't they at least give us a credit toward repair, or actually replace the part, knowing now that they replaced the broken unit with another faulty part?  She said no, they would not.  I indicated to her that they had just earned a bad review if they could not stand by their products and service.

I have now had a second opinion by another company, which not only concluded that the part itself is still under warranty and could be replaced for the cost of labor and new freon (still several thousand dollars), but that the workmanship done by Dependable was indeed shoddy and would need to be redone, now costing us more money to remedy.< /Text>
